Joe believes his hospital's babies weigh more on average than those from Green Veggies.</p><p>Use a one tailed two sample t test for H1: &mu;<sub>Joe</sub> &gt; &mu;<sub>Veggies</sub>.</p><p>Assume unequal variances (Welch's t test).</p><table style='border-collapse:collapse;'><tr><td style='vertical-align:top; padding-right:20px;'><b>Joe's Hospital (lbs):</b><br/><span style='font-family:monospace; background-color:#eee; white-space:pre;'>5.7<br/>9.4<br/>7.8<br/>8.9<br/>7.0<br/>4.6<br/>7.8<br/>8.7<br/>10.5<br/>8.4<br/>5.2<br/>8.5<br/>7.5<br/>8.2<br/>7.7<br/>8.7<br/>7.0<br/>7.3<br/>7.1<br/>9.5<br/>7.8<br/>8.3<br/>9.3<br/>4.2<br/>10.0<br/>7.0<br/>7.9<br/>8.8<br/>4.0<br/>6.5</span></td><td style='vertical-align:top;'><b>Green Veggies (lbs):</b><br/><span style='font-family:monospace; background-color:#eee; white-space:pre;'>9.2<br/>8.5<br/>4.0<br/>7.8<br/>6.1<br/>9.3<br/>6.2<br/>7.4<br/>7.3<br/>7.3<br/>5.9<br/>8.9<br/>4.6<br/>7.0<br/>4.9<br/>11.1<br/>7.3<br/>5.6<br/>7.8<br/>7.5<br/>4.6<br/>8.6<br/>7.3<br/>7.4<br/>7.3<br/>6.1<br/>7.0</span></td></tr></table><p>Compute the p value in Google Sheets using the tutorial: <a href='https://docs.google.com/document/d/1k5UzUlpu-5wCMyWpop0bFlXBgAWivwTwd020Jgo1EIk/edit' target='_blank' rel='noopener'>link here</a>.</p><p>Enter your result as a decimal between 0 and 1 (for example, 0.084, not 8.4%).</p>	0.11089762	0.00110000
